游戲文

老爺經 256

— 愼敏

老爺身分果然高，欺貧重富太驕傲，

威風凛凛神氣足，面孔扳起刮刮呌，

稍有一些不如意，碰檯碰凳擲脚跳，

目高於頂頭寸大，舉止闊綽資格老，

生來本性色情狂，看見女子迷迷笑，

家裏有了賢太太，外面還討幾個小，

舍已耘人更難免，家花那比野花好，

野渡無人舟自横，應接不暇請代表，

現成一頂綠頭巾　，戲在身上發飛跑，

太太面前都瞞過，河東獅吼不得了，

醋瓶打翻難收拾，跪踏板時眞苦惱，

遐邇馳名雌老虎，雌威暴發勢咆哮，

老爺本領雖不小，有法無靈眞倒灶，

揑住鼻子忍耐熬，家醜外揚被人笑，

神氣活現大好老，斡出這樣現世報，

奉勸摩登老爺們，架子不必搭得高，

際兹國難臨頭日，哀鴻遍野正嗷嗷，

富人自應發善心，拯救災難諸同胞，

節省搉霍移助賑，隂功積德名譽高，

踴躍輸將須慷慨，發財發福生意好，

匹夫有責共擔負，挽回刦運身家保。

她不配做我的妻 257

— 敬嘉

自從有了一百五十塊錢一月之後，卞漸漸地厭棄他底妻英了。他對任何親友說：「她不配做我底妻了！這付醜相」

！」於是他把英和一個五歲的孩子丢在鄕下，另外混着一個女人。

說句老實話，英並不醜。當她在娘家過着黃金色的少女生活的時候，有不少的人追求着她。媒人常在她家裏出入着。卞也是追求著她的一個。當時愛着她的還有一個姓陳的。論門户，那姓陳的和卞是不相上下的：論品貌，卞實在比不上那個姓陳的。然而，爲了家庭，爲了環境，勝利終於屬於卞所有了。

我們不難想像到卞那時的喜歡和滿足的情形。當我們得到了我們所願望的東西時是何等的快樂啊！當然，在那時的卞比得到了五十萬的頭奬更爲快樂的。

然而，在「彼一時此一時」的口號之下，卞是遺棄了她了。當然，在不同的環境下是會有不同的慾生的。從前認爲最美的現在也認爲最醜的了。人的心是那樣的不可測摸啊！不是嗎？當卞追求英的時候曾經說過：「我要是没有她，我寗可死。」然而現在他却說：「要是我再和她做夫妻，我不是人養的。」

英有什麽辦法呢？她只能怪自已的命不好。她只能緊緊地抱着那天眞的孩子，把痛苦的涙珠滴在他的臉上。她把她將殘的青春一點一點地消靡掉，在痛苦裏，在寂寞裏。

雖然英的親友爲她不平，但是又有什麽用呢？卞曾經說過：「夫妻之事要絶對的自主，别人無權干預。」雖然英的親友們知道所謂：「絶對自主」的滑稽和矛盾，但是他們都不過是背鋤頭爲人流血汗的農夫而已！對於一個穿洋服掛徵章的官老爺，他們敢怎樣呢？

據說，卞在外面又娶了女人，並且有了兒子了。英的破碎了的心永没有回原的希望。結果她是瘋了！她哭着喊着，披着頭髮從這個村莊跑到那個村莊，又從那個村莊跑到另一村莊。黑暗的世界上又多了一個苦痛的瘋人了。

小說

上海（四） 258

— 張老三

（七）姐姐的靈魂

除了在天的父母，數百里外的可愛的弟弟，我還有同情的敵人，新的開始，没有給我失望，英麗的前程，閃耀着一線光明。我重獲了我的敏姊愛我的敏姊。

十歲時候吧，元宵佳節，父親賈來三個走馬燈，天還没有黑，點上臘獨，姊弟爾個，到處亂跑，弟弟剛會學步，腰裏縛了腰帶，乳母楊媽扶着他，一手提了走馬燈，想跨大步和我們一樣亂跑亂跳。不留神，額角碰着牆壁，弟弟大哭起來；爸媽本來是最痛小弟弟的，知道是我們兩個禍種頭，二個走馬燈被搜去懸在牆壁上不許再玩。敏姊偷偷地拖了我的手說：「大街上有龍燈，魚燈，許許多多的燈，比這兩個走馬燈好玩，我們去看，不要給媽知道」。

我們偷出了門口，滿街上都是人，提着各式各樣的燈，歡躍，狂笑，我們在一家熟識的店門前站定，遠遠地擁來一簇人，混雜的聲音喊着看龍燈看龍燈，人羣像潮比一樣湧來，我們不及避讓，姊弟兩個被捲散了。我一邊湧着走，一邊高聲喊敏姊，這時候誰都没有注意到一個走失姐姐的孩子哭着喊着，我被擠倒在路旁，有一個熟識的人將我帶到家裏…

我受爸爸媽媽一頓重的責打，從此我失去了愛我的敏姊，現在姐姐的靈魂已降臨在頑皮孩子的身上。「我是敏姊」，這有力的細小聲音，給了我更大的勇氣。

我注視着敏姊的臉，敏姊注視着我，房内維持互相領悟的歡悅，兩個異鄕人的心中，激蕩起勝利的凱旋。

（八）春天的上海

從餐室步行着歸來，上海充滿了活躍的空氣，每一個微笑的影子閃耀在霓虹燈的光輝裏。南京路上的窗飾，誘惑行路人的注視，「夢中情人」多情的從無線電中播送出來，黃包夫也放開輕鬱的脚步，拉着他們的主顧到目的地去，在上海，似乎不見一張愁苦的臉。我們跳躍着返旅館。

靠上洋台，遥望迷茫中的故鄕，我記起我可愛的弟弟。

「敏姊，我們到上海來吃苦，不是享樂，住着這樣高貴的旅館，離我們到上海來的宗旨太遠，我們的先决問題丨一所幽靜的寓所，亭子樓也不妨，我們須從底下層做起！」

「弟弟，恕我騙你到這樣的旅館來。我有朋友，是幼稚園的校長，不久以前，她寫信來要我分她一點職務，讓我先去恢復我的音心，整理我的靈魂。你，先見你的舅舅，多少他能帮助你，你别以爲資本家都没有同情。從昨天起這神經惝恍，在火車上你不是没有睡覺嗎，喃喃地自語，我眞怕你要自殺啦，睡罷，本天的上海，晚上還是斜寒襲人」。

「敏姊，我辜負了你的好意，恕我，駡你無靈魂的女人」。

關上了長窗，我脫衣睡穩了，敏姊纔退身出去。疲乏確是疲乏，但被某一種莫明其妙興奮的東西剌激着整個的身體，用數一二三四的催眠法，數目儘自增加，兩眼呆望着帳頂没有睡意。　亂的思潮，更像電影似的閃映：畢業後的朋友都失散了，一個人被遣棄了地歸到故鄕，故鄕對於我並没有可戀的所在，兩位老人家的墳墓，橋下的流水，可愛的弟弟之外，我不願再提及任何一個人及任何東西。現在明知我已投身進了另一個世界，但是一切我不願提及的人物，徧在帳門的四圍不肯離去。重行披衣起身，燃上一枝捲烟，那是敏姊遺留在這裏的，一時我又想到這令人惝惚的女子，從她的叙述裏，她是我母親的寄女無疑，好像比親也對我說過敏妹回來了的話，不過我好像始終没有見過　，而她反這般注意我的行動，…我深深地吸了一口烟，開了長窗。

Page 22

Page 23

電影專刊

南洋巴里風景人物的一斑 259

— 西復

美國的黃金提高了當地的生活　弄得别國人起了望洋興歎之感

我記得前幾年有一個奥國的油糧家到了上海，他因爲朋友的介紹，讀我到他的寓所褒看他在南海一個巴里（Ｂali）島上的作品。我是早已聽見過巴里這個島，它在我的腦筋裏，如同夏威夷一樣具有使我「心嚮往之」的吸力。因爲那處山水幽美，人物秀麗，老實說，尤其是那種「本天眞而不着上衣的女子。可是那位美術家况給了我一個更深刻的了解，他的作品竟没有一張裸體的女子，而竟是一個一個端莊無比的女子正面面容。我在他的作品中，認爲巴里女子面貌之美，是世界各國女子所不及的，不能拿搽些香粉，點些臙脂的摩登女子去比擬的。拿塗脂抹粉的女子，和巴里的天然秀色相比，猶之以泥塑木雕的偶像，比之於團城玉佛的莊嚴妙相也。

但是這和電影有什麽關係呢？我的感想是由於一個消息而起的。我聽到好萊塢已經派人到巴里拍了一張完全當地風光的影片。我欣喜我們將來有在銀幕上看到巴里人物風景的希望，但是我國爲不願意作事先的過份宣傳，所以片名等等，暫時不提了。

大家恐怕都知道南洋羣島的名字，在英文上那個地方呌　南海（ＳouthSeas）。那地雄中國並不遠。那里最大的一個島呌做婆羅洲，那是英國的屬地。再望南就是爪哇，巴里等地，統通是荷屬東印度的地方。我們中國人在那裡經商貿易的極多，很操縱商業上一大部份的勢力。但是那裡，尤其係巴里，因爲白人知道的很少，所以除掉土人和中國人之外，白人去游歷的很少。聽說在五年前，歐美人士到巴里去游歷的，平均每季不過七十人。可是　了現在，每季歐美人士前往游歷的，竟增加到一千五百人之多，於是荷蘭政府竟在游歷事業上面，大大的發了一筆財。

我們都知道荷蘭國的政府，是靠殖民地發財的，這點對於巴里尤其眞確。巴里這個島，係由荷蘭政府將那裡的專利權賣給一個公司的，而荷蘭國的王后就是那個公司的大股東之一。自從美國人發見了那地方的風景人物之後，他們都拿它當作神仙樂土，都上那裡去游歷，尤其是好萊塢的明星們。自從美國人拿他們的黃金，在那裡誇耀過之後，那裏的生活標凖，就和那里的熱度一樣高升到了極頂。恐怕英法的富人，還可以到那里賞鑒賞鑒不穿上衣的少女。别國的人，恐怕就有望塵莫及之歎。聽說荷蘭人自已都不肯去的，因爲物價太高了。

好萊塢的明星們，到那裡去游歷的眞不少。其中頂有名的是却利卓别靈范朋克等等。　有一個笑話，就是却利卓别靈和他的兄弟雪特到了那裡，當地的荷蘭政府，不知爲什麽緣故，竟拿他當作兩位皇帝降臨看待，天天請他們游玩，吃飯，弄得他們啼笑不得，弄出胃病出來。後來幸虧一位老朋友把他們救了出來，藏在島邊的一個荒僻地方，繼拿胃病養好。而現在在巴里游玩的有格蘿利亞史璜和她的丈夫享利，以及康絲登斯義納脫等人。

影片談評

評「香草美人」 260

— 凌鶴

丨明星出品丨新光開映丨

首先我們得承認作者採取現實的題材，而正確的把握和分析，的確是難能可貴的。

農村破産，鄕間的男女不斷的擠到都市擠入工廠，這是必然的現象。但是所謂民族資本終於敵不過外國資本的侵略，在竭盡棉力的競爭之下，到底失敗了。同時，民族資本雖然屈服於外國的經濟或政治的淫威之卜，另一方面却從工人身上盡量的壓迫榨取。因此，工人們飢餓，痛苦，工廠關門之後，社會上的失業者日益增加。這時候，覺悟者爲生活掙扎，奮門。反之，「純良忠厚」的工人們！安分守已的結果，使他們在極度磨折之後，亦認識了自身的出路。

全般的說，我們很同意劇作者的說法，不過其中對於民族資本的愛憐，與其後來又寫到工人生活因被剥削而處於死境，未免顯示作者情感上的矛盾。我們在作品中，固然應當寫出民族資本必然的没落，然而過於同惰却减弱了觀衆的情感，這不能不是一種損失吧？據說這一影片的劇本是一個復旦大學學生編製的，這是更加感覺興趣。的確，中國電影已經廣泛的被一般人所注意了，而且有着這種新的傾向和良好的成績，更證明中國電影前途的偉大。

在演出方面，導演陳鏗然君以現在和回憶相互的運用，在中國總算是一種新的方法。不過我們覺得過於用多了，却使人嫌其片斷的而破壞了情調上的統一性，有如流水賬似的。譬如說王阿大在法庭上說，「這樣又過了三年」，或是「有一天晚上，」馬上再以畫說明，這對於演出未管不是一種方便的方法，然而假使很有組織的將畫面嚴密的編織起來，也不是没有可能，而且觀衆的情感更因之緊凑而統一。我們以爲開頭的法庭，由巡捕口中變爲畫面，直至阿大說「我是一個木匠……」爲止，立刻完全以畫面叙述到底，最後再在法庭上終止這一回憶，似乎比較的很好。何况一段往事，又一段法庭，到底使人厭煩。而且總說明的字幕也覺過多。

除此以外，我們得承認導演者是相當運用了新的方法的。對於夏佩珍所飾的王阿大的女兒之性格的描畫，用香水，新旗袍，學抽香煙等等，以說明她以後大胆的出賣肉體，對於王微信所飾的阿大之兄弟，以工作時吃茶的敢怒而不敢言，而說明他反抗的個性，對於謝雲卿所飾的阿大，更是唯愼唯謹的而使他代表封建錢餘時代的典型人物。以及其他幾個演員的選擇，如阿大的老婆之純粹的賢妻，（其偕女兒出走，却有點奇突。）那個孩子的營養不良，都是很好的。

還有應該指出的，如窗外的夜景，自黑夜至天明，由於女兒的香煙而發現女兒帶了男人到家，在工塲中騷動的場面，巡捕捉阿大和其兄弟的場面，燒乳糕，阿大逗孩兒等等，都是很好的。特别是關於王阿大一家的描寫，都充滿了眞正的中國人的生活習慣。還有金元打倒中國煙囱的「卡通」，也是好的。

然而也有好些小的缺點：寫阿大之妻出走，前面没有相當伏線的描寫，以致奇突。在遊戲場中的許多鏡頭，佔了時間太多。阿大抱孩子到醫院去的一段路景，大可省掉，然而回來的路景却有意義了。同時悲劇的情感也嫌不夠，這應當是前面所說的法庭場面的破壞，因爲不能集中感覺的原故。

現在再要說到演員了。謝雲卿的成績，簡直使人驚奇。在「鐵板紅涙錄」中那樣失敗，而在這裏印是如此成功。他對於劇中人的感情，個性，眞是太有把握了。這一影片能有如此成績，他照當第一居功。夏佩珍從樓上下來慢慢的扣着衣領，非常自然，可是較之已往却未見進步。特别是她的頭部化裝，更覺不宜。王微信比較以前演得好多了。自「鐵板紅涙錄」中他開始飾反抗的角色以後，這裏確表現出他的成績。最好的自然是吃茶的那一個鏡頭。

攝影雖不見精采，也還可以，這在大公司中是不足　奇的。佈景犯了和以前同樣的毛痢，如法庭和置院等，弄得那末現代化，總使人感覺太隔閡，爲什麽要在佈景上來努力於劇情没有必要的誇張呢？希望明星公司的裝置家特别注意。

評「健美的女性」 261

— 李馥

據寡聞的筆者的記憶，這是在一海開映的第一張没有故事的「純文化電影。」丨丨幾年前在北四川路日本演藝館開映而被當時的上海人哄傳做模特兒影片的「産婦衛生影片」，雖然可以說是文化電影的一種，但是純客觀的「記錄電影」與具備着積極的敎育意義的「文化電影」之間，是有相當距離的差别的。

雖則在報紙上，不曾指出這是那一國的出品，但是，祇要稍稍留心一點世界文化電影情形的人們，誰都知道這是一張蘇聯梅奇拉姆社的作品。丨丨一張蘇聯影片上映的時候，竟用「意大利墨索里尼，德國希德拉奬勵」等字樣來作宣傳，這不能不令人感到異樣的滑稽。其實在德國，包含着文化電影在内的一切蘇聯電影，早已被希德拉政府禁止的了。

這片子是在一定的目的意識之下，用記錄電影的方法，加上很多巧妙的圖解線盡而編攝的作品，爲着調劑觀衆興味，中間還夾寫了幾段顯明的對比，譬如蒙古民族在分娩時的那種懷無人進，而又使人發噱的習慣，在這兒拿來和蘇聯政府經營的勞働婦人産院的一切設備比擬一下，這不僅很有效的達到敎育的目的，而且，對於那種能使一切女性那般舒適而又安心地逐行母性天職的社會組織，發生一種深刻的反省。

我們看到了工場女工的衛生設備。在工作幾小時之後，女工們很愉快地打開了一切窗户，脫去了工作衣服，整齊地舉行五分鐘的柔軟

幾乎使我懷疑，以爲這是和「小玩意」裡面的黎莉莉敎貧苦兒童們學體操一樣的是一種作者的空想；在我　後的一位觀客就在悄悄地說：「這是實際上叢不到的事情」。不錯，在中國或歐美日本，這確是做不到的，可是在這片子上所表示的，原是在另一　社會秩序下的蘇聯。曾有這樣的一句名言：「電影在愚昧的欺許者手裡的時候，非特不能使觀衆得到好處，而且要對他們散播着有害的種子，可是當觀衆自已獲得了電影的時候，當電影被把握在新文化的眞實的活動者的掌中的時候，它就變成大衆敎育的一種最有力的工具。」「健美的女性」，證實了這句話的正確，這片子可以使觀衆得到很多的好處，不論在智識上，在認識上。

這片子和那些爲着營利而製作使觀衆發生不良的作品，比較一下，我想聰明的觀衆，一定能夠得到一個明　的答案吧。

我們的金燄　原來如此！ 262

— 鶴

說也奇怪，在霞飛路上我遇着了金燄了。爲什麽奇怪呢？這是没有理由的。在我，總算是奇遇。我們不是長久不見面了麽。現在又遇着了。

只見他穿了一件紅色羊毛上衣，打哥爾夫球穿的西裝褲頭上是小學生戴的帽子。不大健康的臉色，十足的黃種典型。我們拉了一次手。我說：

「我看了報上你登的啟事，到底是怎麽事呀？」

「這個嗎，說起來眞是笑話，有人把我看成某黨某派的要人了，這簡直太誇大我了。事實上小子無知，一無所長，慚愧得很，只能在銀幕上給女人們開開心。所以登一個啟事，說幾句老實話。」

「嗄，這眞是太……太……太什麽了（一個人詞不達意總是很苦的。）可是什麽有人疑到你的頭上來呢？」

「這大概是因爲在南國社演過卡門的原因」又是他說：「可是這也是非常簡單的事。田漢敎萬籟天來找我帮忙演戲，我爲了自已歡喜便來了一次。其實我和田漢根本就没有什麽交情，他家裏我也不知道在什麽地方。」

「唔，這才滑稽了。……」我再問。「那末你演「母性之光」，「三個摩登女性」那種片子，也是容易給人悮會的囉。」

「老兄，這也是没有辦法的事。老實說，我到底是一演員，我和公司裡訂了合同，公司要我演那一個角色，我能夠不答應嗎？他們要我做賣國的奸臣，我也不得不幹啊。」

「不說了罷，這些事情。……你近來的生活怎樣」

「我的生活嗎，總算是滿有味的。我星期三和星期六學聲樂。此外打球，翻槓子，發粉盡，看電影，還歡喜打獵。說到這裡我又要說了。一個電影演員，他的面孔一定是大家認識的，我到那裡也没有方法秘密，像我這樣的人，還配秘密活動？」

「哦！原來如此。」

一輛汽車駛來，將我們左右分開，就此我向他揚揚手，說：

「你去你的罷，我得回去了。」

電影小說爲國爭光（二） 263

— 謝月笙

「姐姐，他是剛打城裏來的·」紅玉連忙凑上去替天雄辯答，一面向他哥哥丢了一個眼色，故意把那件坎肩給雪芳看。「姐姐：你看這是他剛從城裏買來的。」她很公平地替她哥哥解釋。雪芳感覺自已說話太冒失，頓時臉上起了一陣紅暈。天雄也怕她誤會，就把城裏聽得的新聞講給她倆聽。他告訴雪芳，明天西湖邊將要舉行一個美術展覽大會，約會她明日一同去參觀。雪芳很爽直的答應了。

第二天的早晨，雪芳偕着天雄紅玉，在展覽會裏，參觀那位藝術家蘇容的作品。蘇容親自招待。他是個年少有爲的藝術家。風度瀟洒，談吐温和，在愛美心理高漲的雪芳，經過了這次的認識，使她内心的深處，糾起一度劇烈的叛變。她告訴他住址，說她家裏祇有一個老母同一個弱妺。以一個客鄕孤獨的蘇容，偶然地得到了這個意外的奇遇，當然很高興的接受了。「蘇先生有空請到舍間去，再會吧！」雪芳天雄紅玉向蘇容道别了，蘇容親自送了他們出來。

「梅小姐也在這裏嗎？」這陣聲音把雪芳衆人楞住了。於是大家把視線注意到這個人身上去，只見那人大摇大擺地走了過來。雪芳認得他是當地很有財勢的紳士曹懷仁，但她厭惡他那種驕慢無禮的舉動，勉强地招呼了他一聲，逕自去了。曹懷仁恃着金錢萬能，就實行他的追求工作。過工幾天？曹懷仁特地買了許多禮物，去謁訪梅雪芳。

「她有病醫生說不能見客，」曹懷仁竟遭擋駕了。但他並不懷疑她，祇是很掃興地出來了。這不是那天展覽會裏的少年美術家蘇容嗎嗎？曹懷仁看見了蘇容走進梅家去，頓時會悟到自已當時被擋駕的情形來。他决定進去探明個眞相。

一嘔，你就是蘇先生嗎？請坐！小女在裏頭哪。」懷仁聽見這個說話人的聲音，正是剛才和自已說話的那個中年婦人。於是他的呼吸也短促了，手足也發頗了。他知道那個少年美術家無疑地是自已的情敵了。他不忍再聽下去，就悄悄地退了出來。在外面換吸了一口氣，懊喪地走了。恰巧紅玉和天雄同來訪雪芳，她看見曹懷仁從裡面出來，忙着向天雄說：「哥哥：你看那人怎麽也來看梅小姐呢？」

一我看他不像好人，梅小姐怎麽也和他往來哪？」他倆同樣地怎樣想，一面已走　梅家去了。（未完）

1933.11.27

The Zhejiang Border Defenses are Strengthened; Shouning, Fuding, and Other Counties Show No Traces of the Fujian Army; Lu Dipin and Liu Heding Negotiate Concrete Coordination; Liu, Lu, and Zhou's Troops Gradually Retreat Temporarily Toward the Zhejiang Border 1

(Wenzhou) Shouning, Fuding, and other counties currently show no traces of the Fujian army. (26th Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Lu Dipin sent representatives to the Fujian border to meet with Liu Heding to discuss joint methods for suppressing Fujian. Liu expressed his determination to take consistent action with the Central Government and Zhejiang Province, and also sent representatives to Zhejiang to meet with Lu, hoping to establish concrete coordination with Zhejiang Province. Lu Xingbang and Zhou Ziqun's troops are still stationed in northern Fujian. Zhejiang Province has also made contact, and the Zhejiang border defense is becoming increasingly substantial. The current situation is extremely stable. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Liu Heding, Lu Xingbang, and Zhou Ziqun's troops, unwilling to associate with the Fujian side, are now gradually retreating temporarily toward the Zhejiang border, so as to establish contact with the National Army and the Zhejiang Army, and then await orders to advance. After Liu and others were met by Ling Peng, dispatched by Lu Dipin, they decided to take consistent action with Zhejiang. Liu and others also sent representatives to accompany Lu's representatives to the province to meet with Lu. They are expected to arrive in Hangzhou today. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Main Fleet Standing By For Departure 2

(Nanjing) Military News: Following the Fujian Incident, Naval Commander Chen Shaokuan, recognizing the importance of naval defense, has been planning at the ministry for days. He has specifically dispatched Vice Minister Li Shijia to Shanghai to summon senior naval officers to discuss and arrange naval defenses. After Li Shijia arrived in Shanghai and conferred with First Fleet Commander Chen Jiliang for several days, he telegraphed the Torpedo Guerrilla Fleet's Wang Shouting, the Training Fleet's Chen Xunyong, and others on the 25th to go to Shanghai to discuss matters. Wang and Chen both went to Shanghai on the evening of the 25th and arrived at the First Fleet Headquarters at Gaochang Temple on the morning of the 26th for a meeting. As for the warships dispatched from Shanghai yesterday to patrol and blockade the Min River, there are three ships including the Yongxu and Yongjian. Currently, the main fleet's Ninghai, Hairong, Haichou, Datong, Xianning, and more than ten other ships are still concentrated and anchored outside the Wusong Estuary, awaiting orders. Once the plan is finalized, the three commanders, Chen Jiliang, Wang Shouting, and Chen Xunyong, will separately lead the fleet to patrol key ports in Fujian and Zhejiang and deploy defenses accordingly. Li Mengbin, commander of the key port of Mawei, is still awaiting orders in Sandu Ao. As for the naval infantry stationed in Fujian, some have escaped and are advancing towards Sandu Ao in succession. (26th Dispatch)

Chiang Sends Planes to Fujian, Warning the 19th Route Army: "The False Government Will Be Bombed Flat Within Days. Return Quickly, or Jade and Stone Will Perish Together." 3

(Nanchang) Chiang has been sending planes to Fujian for days to scatter leaflets to the 19th Route Army, stating that he is determined to bomb the Fujian false government flat within days. He hopes they will return quickly, otherwise jade and stone will perish together. (26th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) It is proclaimed here that the government is simultaneously suppressing the communists and rebelling against the insurgents. (25th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Due to the Fujian affair, Chiang has ordered all units in eastern Jiangxi to intensify their blockade against the Red bandits. (25th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Fearing that the bandits might take advantage of the Fujian Incident to steal and attack, the Jiangxi Provincial Joint Communist Suppression Association resolved on the 24th to send a telegram to the Central Government, reaffirming its determination to diligently suppress the communists. (25th Dispatch)

The People's Government Appoints a Large Number of Personnel 4

(Xiamen) On the 24th, the People's Government appointed Feng Yuxiang as Chairman of the Economic Committee, to be replaced by Yu Qingxin before his arrival, and Huang Qixiang as Director of the Counselors Corps. (25th Dispatch)

(Xiamen) At the second meeting of various committees on the 24th, it was decided to appoint Peng Zexiang as Secretary-General of the People's Government, Cai Tingkai as Commander-in-Chief of the First Front Army and concurrently Commander-in-Chief of the 19th Route Army, Deng Shizeng as Deputy Commander, Shen Guanghan as Commander of the First Army, Li Chengzong as Deputy, Mao Weishou as Commander of the Second Army, Zhang Li as Deputy, Qu Shounian as Commander of the Third Army, Huang Gu as Deputy, Zhang Yan as Commander of the Fourth Army, Tan Qixiu as Commander of the Fifth Army, Liu Zhanxiong as Commander of the First Division, Pang Cheng as Commander of the Second Division, Zhang Junsong as Commander of the Third Division, Xie Qiongsheng as Commander of the Fourth Division, Situ Guang as Commander of the Fifth Division, Ruan Baohong as Commander of the 49th Division, Deng Shicai as Commander of the 60th Division, Liang Shiji as Commander of the 61st Division, Yun Yinglin as Commander of the 78th Division, Zhao Yijian as Commander of the Seventh Division. They were sworn into office on the 25th. Qiu Zhaochen was transferred to command the Vanguard Force. Qiu Guozhen succeeded as Director of the Fuzhou Public Security Bureau. The Zhangzhou headquarters was closed and a military headquarters was established, with Xie Dongshan as director. A military headquarters was established in Yanping, with Deng Shizeng as director. (25th Dispatch)

Wealthy Families in Zhangzhou and Xiamen are Fleeing to Hong Kong and Macau 5

(Hong Kong) Wealthy families in Zhangzhou and Xiamen have been fleeing to Hong Kong and Macau in recent days. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Fujian Invites Guangxi to Participate; Li and Bai Ignore It 6

(Nanjing) The Fujian side invited Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi of Guangxi to participate in the call to action. According to a certain important person associated with Li and Bai, a telegram has been received from Guangxi stating that Li and Bai believe that at this time of serious concern, they should be rectifying the interior in order to seek salvation. They believe that Chen Mingshu and others' actions this time are unnecessary blind adherence and are ignoring it. (26th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Huang Jianping, the representative of Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi, arrived in Nanjing by boat on the 26th after meeting with Chiang in Jiangxi. Huang said that Li and Bai are quite disapproving of the Fujian false organization and have decided not to join it. They also expressed their adherence to the same attitude as Guangdong Province, obeying the orders of the highest party and government organs in the Southwest, and working hard to suppress bandits and defend the country. He himself had reported this intention when he met with Chiang in Jiangxi. (26th Dispatch)

Chen Jitang Sends Chen Qingyun to Beijing to Discuss All Strategies for Blockading Fujian 7

(Nanjing) Since the Fujian Incident, Chen Jitang has sent Yang Dezhao to contact the Central Government repeatedly to discuss response strategies. Yang has already flown to Jiangxi to meet with Chiang to report on the latest preparations for Guangdong-Fujian border defense and the attitude of Guangxi Province, and to discuss all strategies for dealing with the Fujian situation with the Central Government. He has also sent Central Committee member Chen Qingyun to the north. Chen arrived in Beijing on the morning of the 26th and immediately visited important figures in the Central Government. He will stay in Beijing for a few days and then travel to Jiangxi. (26th Dispatch)

Yan Expresses Disapproval of the Fujian Incident; Sends Secret Telegrams Separately to Wang and Chiang 8

(Nanjing) After the Fujian Incident, the Central Government sent telegrams to all parties, reporting the true situation. Yesterday, Yan Xishan of Taiyuan sent secret telegrams separately to Wang and Chiang, expressing his disapproval of the disturbances in Fujian Province, saying that during this period of domestic and foreign troubles, such a phenomenon of division and secession should not occur, and measures should be taken to stop it immediately to prevent the recurrence of war. (26th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yan's representative, Jia Deyao, passed through Ping on the 26th on his way to Tianjin. (26th Dispatch)

All Parties Denounce the Fujian Rebellion 9

(Beiping) The 12 party branches of North China held a joint meeting yesterday and decided to send a telegram to the Central Government to sanction the Fujian Incident. (26th Jiji Dispatch)

(Hankou) On the 26th, He Chengjun replied to Liu Zhenhua, echoing the telegram to suppress Fujian and resolving to advocate unity. (26th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Overseas Chinese Songhu Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Army Association telegraphed Chairman Chiang, requesting him to immediately issue a clear order to suppress Chen Mingshu and others for the Fujian Incident. The original telegram is as follows: (Omissions) Your Excellency leads a mighty army to encircle and suppress the communist bandits. The great scourge in the heartland is gradually being pacified. The whole country is grateful and yearns for governance. The turning point for national prosperity is here. However, at this time of national crisis, when the nation is on the verge of destruction, rebellious party members Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, Cai Tingkai, and others dare to raise the banner of rebellion, openly betray the party and the country, sell out the nation, sell supplies to the bandits, and collude with enemy countries. The bad news has spread, and all Chinese are ashamed. Such rebels must be severely apprehended, or where will party discipline and national law exist? We comrades are deeply saddened and are determined to wait for orders and serve as vanguards, vowing to slaughter the great criminals and calm the public's anger. We earnestly request an immediate clear order to suppress and sweep away the evil forces in order to glorify the party and the country. We cannot express the urgency of waiting for orders in this telegram. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Overseas Chinese Songhu Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Army Association issued the following statement to overseas compatriots regarding the Fujian Incident: To overseas newspaper offices and organizations, and to all compatriots around the world: At this time when bandit suppression is steadily succeeding and the nation is gradually being restored, a gang of rebellious party members, Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, Cai Tingkai, and others, are colluding with the Third Party, the Social Democratic Party, and all reactionary, corrupt, and frivolous politicians, holding the 19th Route Army hostage, openly betraying the party and the country, organizing a false People's Government, colluding with enemy countries, supplying bandits with supplies, endangering the nation, bringing shame to the outside world, and being insane and beastly. What is even more painful is that the aircraft and war equipment that overseas Chinese purchased with blood and sweat and donated to the army during the Battle of Shanghai were originally hoped to be able to thoroughly resist Japan and be used to defend the country, but now they are being used by rebels to harm the nation. Alas, how painful! The country is precarious and cannot withstand further chaos. Our association leads overseas Chinese at home and abroad to engage in the national rejuvenation movement and to implement the principles of domestic pacification and foreign resistance. All rebels are considered enemies. In addition to summoning comrades and telegraphing Chairman Chiang to be prepared for battle, we especially express our sincerity and earnestly hope that all patriotic overseas Chinese will unanimously denounce them, understanding that with the country in danger, we have an inescapable responsibility to ensure that this motley crew of ugly creatures is wiped out completely in the shortest possible time, so that the nation may have a chance to rise and our suffering may be relieved. We cannot express the anger and urgency in this telegram. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Hu Hanmin and Others Telegraph Fujian to Uphold Justice, Sharply Criticize Leaving the Party and Alliance with the Communists, and State That They Cannot Condone Absurd Actions and Still Hope For a Change of Heart to Consolidate Southwest Unity 10

(Guangzhou) Hu Hanmin, Xiao Focheng, and others sent a telegram to Chen, Li, and others in Fujian Province on the 24th, saying: Chen Zhenru, Li Renchao, Jiang Jingran, Cai Xianchu brothers, greetings, your telegram has been received. (Omission) News has spread that you brothers held a meeting in Fujian and declared your secession from the Chinese Kuomintang, abolition of the Blue Sky White Sun flag, approached Japan externally, colluded with the communists internally, and issued a political program openly calling for the overthrow of party rule and the organization of a government of peasants and workers. Initially, it was thought that with the brothers' past history in the party, they would not regress to such an extent. However, newspaper reports clearly indicate that the news is true. This is not only providing an excuse for those who rebel against the party and sell the country, but also causing the brothers' past history of resisting Japan, suppressing communists, protecting the party, and saving the country to be completely erased. Moreover, it is betraying principles, inviting external invasion, and fanning the flames of communism, causing endless harm. How can such absurd actions gain sympathy at home and abroad? Standing from the position of the Three Principles of the People, not to mention that we cannot condone them, we deeply regret that the brothers have completely abandoned what they have upheld. (Omission) The entire corps of officers of the 19th Route Army have long shared hardships with us brothers. Over the years, they have been inspired by the teachings of the Three Principles of the People and have fought for the party, risking their lives. Their great achievements are admired both at home and abroad. They should still have a deep understanding of justice and not abandon themselves, associating with the communist party and plunging themselves into a dead end. We sincerely hope that the brothers will uphold the spirit of protecting the party and saving the country as in the past, change course, and persuade them in various ways to avoid entering the wrong path, so that the unity of the Southwest can be consolidated and the great cause of saving the country can be promoted. Otherwise, giving others an opportunity will inevitably cause pain to those close and joy to those who hate. Saving the country but harming the country, loving the people but harming the people, we believe that this is definitely not the brothers' original intention. Brothers, for the sake of the party and the country, we must implement our principles and work together. We only hope that the brothers will consider this. We cannot express the urgency of waiting for orders in this telegram. Hu Hanmin, Xiao Focheng, Deng Zeru, Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, Bai Chongxi, Zou Lu. (26th Dispatch)

Southern Jiangxi to be Garrisoned by Hunan Army 11

(Hong Kong) After meeting with He Jian, Chen Jitang returned to the province with a Hunanese councilor. Chen and He agreed that Guangdong, if necessary, would withdraw the garrison troops from southern Jiangxi to defend the Dong River, and southern Jiangxi would be garrisoned by troops dispatched by Hunan. (26th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Chen Jitang's representative in Beijing stated that Chen's flight from Shaoguan to Lechang was purely to discuss with He Jian, Commander-in-Chief of the Western Route Bandit Suppression, how the two provinces could jointly resolve the communist bandit problem. As for how to prepare for the Fujian Incident, Yang Dezhao has already gone to Chairman Chiang to ask for instructions. Chiang personally instructed him and told him to report to Liu Xiang for compliance. Qiu returned to Hankou on the 26th and will report to Liu. (26th Dispatch)

(Guangzhou) According to news received in Guangzhou, Hunan Province is now actively participating in the military blockade of Fujian. It is reported that He Jian has arrived in Lechang in northern Guangdong and is meeting with military leaders who have rushed there from Guangzhou to discuss the military situation on the Hunan-Guangdong-Fujian border. According to He Jian's representative in Guangzhou, He Jian has placed heavy troops on the Hunan-Jiangxi border, corresponding to the Guangdong side. Reuters reported that a certain important person in Guangzhou borrowed a division commander to lead a guard to Lechang on the 24th of this month to meet with the Chairman of Hunan to discuss the military situation on the Hunan-Guangdong-Fujian border. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Guangzhou Chinese news: Chen Jitang has returned to the province after meeting with He Jian in Lechang. It is reported that it has been agreed that Hunan Province will send heavy troops to southern Jiangxi to replace the Guangdong army, so that the Guangdong army can concentrate on dealing with the Fujian affair. It is also reported that two battalions of the 19th Route Army have been transferred from Xiamen to Zhangzhou. Weng Zhaoyuan is now recruiting bandits and organizing them into the Fujian army. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

Chen Jitang Restores Training Regiments 12

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang has decided to restore a total of three training regiments for each army. (26th Dispatch)

Three Patrol Ships Ready to Depart 13

(Guangzhou) It was learned today that three Chinese patrol ships have received instructions to prepare for departure. It is likely that the Haichen and Zhaohe will go to Shantou, and the Haiqi will be transferred to the Humen Battery. It is rumored that the three ships have sailed out of Huangpu, but Reuters has learned that the three ships are still in Huangpu this morning. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

Various Counties Plan to Expand Air Defense 14

(Guangzhou) Guangdong counties, following the order from the provincial party department and the provincial government to expand national defense, will organize air defense associations and purchase at least one aircraft per county according to the current plan. The fundraising method is to have each family donate one month's rent and each store donate an amount equal to 2% of its registered capital in cash. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

Guizhou Obeys Guangdong's Lead 15

(Guangzhou) Wang Jialie, Chairman of Guizhou Province, telegraphed, stating that Guizhou Province has not been involved in the Fujian Incident and will obey Guangdong's lead in everything. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

Chiang Telegraphed the Central Government to Transfer Personnel Familiar with the Fujian Situation 16

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang, greatly concerned about the Fujian Incident, recognized that Fujian's terrain consists of high mountains and steep ridges and telegraphed the Central Government to instruct personnel familiar with the Fujian situation to go to Jiangxi for inquiries. The Central Party Department has specifically dispatched Zhang Meixi and Lin Yisi, Fujianese officials, to Jiangxi. Zhang and others took a China Aviation plane to Xun on the 26th and transferred to Nanchang. (26th Dispatch)

Taking Over Linyu County Seat, Two Measures Agreed Upon, Japanese Army Preparing to Withdraw at the End of the Month, Takeover Possible in Early Next Month, Chaisan Returns to Ping, Tao and Zhu Arrive at Qinhuangdao 17

(Beiping) Two measures have been agreed upon for the takeover of Linyu County seat: 1. The Japanese army in Yuguan will withdraw completely to Suizhong in early December, and the county seat will be taken over by County Magistrate Yin in mid-December. 2. The puppet Manchukuo organs in the city will be moved out, and suitable houses will be found outside the city to restore the situation before the Japanese army occupied it, and police power will be returned. (26th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Tao Shangming and Zhu Shiqin returned to Qinhuangdao from Yuguan this morning to慰勞(console) the security team. Chaisan, who accompanied Tao and Zhu to Yuguan to assist in the takeover, returned to Ping this afternoon because the negotiations between the two sides were largely completed. (26th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Japanese army stationed in the Yuguan, Qinhuangdao, and Beidaihe areas will withdraw at the end of the month, and the takeover of Yuguan is scheduled for the first of next month. (26th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng talked about the issue of the withdrawal of the Malanlue puppet army, which is currently being negotiated with the Japanese side and has not yet been withdrawn. (26th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Jiji Administrative Commissioner's Office will be established in Tongzhou at the beginning of next month, and Yin Rugeng's inspection period has not yet been determined. (26th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Chaisan stated that regarding the Yuguan takeover issue, since Commissioner Tao and others arrived in Yu and met with Captain Endō, the result has been satisfactory. There should be no problem with the Japanese army evacuating Yuguan. The reason for the delay is that the barracks outside the pass have not been completed. After the completion of the construction, all Japanese and Manchu organs in Yu will be moved out of the pass, and the 14th Brigade of the Kwantung Army will simultaneously withdraw to Jinzhou. The garrison army will still be stationed as before in accordance with the Boxer Protocol. The takeover of Yuguan is scheduled to begin in early or mid-December. After Tao obtained this result, he left Yu last night with Section Chief Zhu for Qinhuangdao, inspected there, stayed overnight, and went to Luanzhou today. He will also go to Funing and other places to console the Chinese security team, and then return to Ping to report on the process. (26th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Japanese military officer Chaisan returned to Ping at noon on the 26th. Tao Shangming and Zhu Shiqin went to Qinhuangdao and Changli to console the security team. The procedures for the Yuguan takeover have been negotiated, and the takeover will begin on the first day. After the Endō unit of the Japanese army stationed in Yu withdraws outside the pass, the Wakamatsu Regiment will remain in place for the time being. The organs established by other puppet organizations will be canceled after our takeover. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

The Central Government Intends to Formulate a Solution to the Tibet Problem; Shi Qingyang Discusses With the Dalai Lama's Representatives in Beijing 18

(Nanjing) Regarding the issue of Tibet, the Central Government intends to formulate principles, and the Mongolian-Tibetan Affairs Commission and the Border Affairs Group of the General Staff are drafting measures. Due to the recent situation in Tibet and the Dalai Lama's intentions, they still need to be taken into account. Therefore, Shi Qingyang has invited Gongjue Zhongni, Awang Jianzan, Awang Zaba, and Batu Tandan, four representatives of the Dalai Lama in Beijing, to meet at the commission on the afternoon of the 27th to inquire about the situation in Tibet and show them the solutions proposed by the Central Government. He will ask Gongjue to telegraph the Dalai Lama to solicit his opinion. (26th Dispatch)

Sheng Shicai Telegraphed That the Situation in Xinjiang Province is Dangerous; Ma Zhongying Colludes With Hui King No. 2 19

(Nanjing) Military authorities received a telegram from Sheng Shicai stating that Ma Zhongying is colluding with Hui King Nie Zier to restrain the Chan troops and the situation is dangerous. He requested that a telegram be sent to stop this to avoid the expansion of the situation. In addition, Liu Wenlong and Sheng Shicai jointly telegraphed the Executive Yuan, proposing to issue 2 million yuan in Xinjiang provincial bonds for wartime emergencies and to subsidize administrative expenses. (26th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Liu Wenlong and Sheng Shicai telegraphed Beijing on the 25th, stating that Ma Zhongying secretly sent his deputy division commander Ma Heying to Ashan to coerce the good people and invade Elang Tacheng. Shicai then led a large army out of the province to suppress them and defeated Ma Heying's troops who had fled to Elang Tacheng. The remnant bandits fled. Ma Heying, seeing our army approaching his nest, sent a letter requesting Shicai and expressing his willingness to obey orders, withdraw from Tushan, and go to the designated Hami to station troops. Wenlong believed that everyone wants to be good, so why not me? If things can be resolved, why not compromise? So he discussed with Shicai to withdraw the army back to the province and set a deadline for departure. For two weeks, Ma Heying not only did not withdraw a step from Tushan, but also instigated his ugly creatures to rob and plunder in Fugu in the east and Jingsha in the west, causing counties to suffer damage. His insidious and ferocious nature is intent on destroying the border situation. In order to protect the territory and defend the people, Shicai had to send troops again to punish them. Now the bandits in the east and west are gradually being eliminated, and he will soon lead the team to Hami to suppress the bandits, eliminate the harmful horses, clear out the bandits, relieve the people from their suffering, and relieve the Central Government from its concern. (26th Dispatch)

Fujian Seizes Tax Revenue; The National Treasury is Not Affected 20

(Nanjing) According to information from the Ministry of Finance, the Fujian Customs collects 500,000 yuan per month. The province's salt tax, land tax, and other income are managed independently by the local authorities and there are no precise statistics, but it is estimated to be several hundred thousand yuan per month. However, the central allocation and expenses for the 19th Route Army exceeded 500,000 yuan per month. After the Fujian Incident, these payments were suspended. Therefore, Fujian's seizure of the central government's organs in Fujian has no impact on the central government's fiscal revenue. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) An official from the Customs Administration stated that Fujian originally had Xiamen and Fuzhou Customs and Sandu Ao sub-customs under the jurisdiction of Fujian Customs. The total income of the three customs offices is about 6 million yuan per year, averaging about 500,000 yuan per month, accounting for one-fiftieth of the national customs revenue. The false organization of Fujian Province also sent Chen Youren to negotiate with the Customs Commissioner to request the takeover of Xiamen and Fuzhou Customs. The Customs Commissioner immediately telegraphed Director-General Meller and asked for instructions, and Meller forwarded the matter to Finance Minister Kong for approval. The authorities are considering response measures, but the administration of the two customs offices has not changed as of today. Based on the current situation, if the Fujian Incident cannot be resolved in the short term, the income of the three Fujian customs offices may inevitably be seized. (26th Dispatch)

Huang Shaoxiong Scheduled to Leave Sui for Ping; Mongolian-Han Joint Celebration Postponed 21

(Beiping) Huang Shaoxiong telegraphed He, stating that he is scheduled to leave Sui for Ping on the 30th. (26th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Wu Hueling came to Ping from eastern Chahar and is scheduled to return to Beijing within one or two days to report on everything. According to reports, the principles for the solution to the Inner Mongolia autonomy problem have been decided in Bailingmiao. The principles for the solution is to establish the Inner Mongolia Autonomous Region Government, with Chahar as the first district and Suiyuan as the second district, without changing the original organization of provinces and counties. The district government will be based on the past administrative system and will be directly under the Central Government, and the Central Government will allocate funds to assist it. Regarding local tax revenue, it will be evenly distributed with provinces and counties in the future. The detailed rules of the district government will be decided after Huang returns to Beijing. Fu is quite in favor of the principles of the district government. The Mongolian-Han Joint Celebration has been slightly postponed because the representatives of various leagues and banners have not yet arrived. However, it can be officially opened this month. The representatives of the leagues and banners of Chahar Province have already gone to Sui to participate. They also strongly agree with the principles for organizing the autonomous region government agreed upon in Bailingmiao. Huang Shaoxiong plans to come to Ping on the 28th or 29th. The two kings, Yun and De, each returned to their original banners on the 21st and 22nd of this month. (26th Dispatch)

Salt Merchants' Guild Petition: Safeguarding Salt Affairs Sovereignty - Administrative and Auditing Agencies Should Be Established Separately 25

(Nanjing) The National Salt Merchants' Guild has petitioned the Executive Yuan, requesting that the Ministry of Finance be ordered to separately establish the Salt Affairs Bureau and the Salt Affairs Auditing Office to safeguard sovereignty. The petition states that since Yuan Shikai's large-scale foreign loans, a special Salt Affairs Auditing Office was established, headed by foreign advisors recommended by creditor nations, to supervise revenue and expenditure for debt repayment. However, China still maintained administrative power over salt affairs, with officials such as salt commissioners and deputy commissioners of various provinces still appointed by the government. Around 1925 and 1927, in accordance with Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, efforts were initiated to abolish unequal treaties, starting with the abolition of auditing offices in Guangdong, Hubei, Hunan, and Jiangxi provinces, dismissal of foreign advisors, and recovery of sovereignty. Subsequently, salt affairs bureaus were established in these provinces, handling auditing matters independently and achieving remarkable results without foreign interference. In 1928, due to further foreign loans, the Ministry of Finance restored the auditing offices that had been recovered, causing national outcry and repeated calls for maintaining the old system. However, due to the urgent need for military expenses during the Northern Expedition, the people reluctantly endured this for a time. After national unification, requests for abolishing the auditing offices were renewed. Unfortunately, last year, Zhu Tingqi, the chief of the Auditing Office, had the Salt Affairs Bureau merged into the Auditing Office, and the powers of salt commissioners were also incorporated into the Office's scope. This was tantamount to handing over the remaining administrative power over salt affairs. Merchants and civilians are running around in fear and confusion. Furthermore, placing administration and auditing in one agency is prone to corruption. The current prevalence of smuggled salt is a direct result of this. The petition requests that national rights and people's livelihoods be protected, the hardships of merchants be considered, and the Ministry of Finance be ordered to separately establish the two agencies, gradually recovering the auditing power over salt affairs. This would be fortunate for the nation and its merchants and people. (26th Dispatch)

French Ship Henri Attacked En Route from Hong Kong to Haiphong: 15,000 Yuan Worth of Goods Looted, Four Chinese Passengers Abducted 31

(Hong Kong) Another case of a foreign ship encountering pirates has occurred in the South China Sea. A few days ago, the police station issued a wireless warning that many bandits had departed from Dapeng Bay and crossed the British territory border with the intention of robbery. Although ships had taken extra precautions, the French ship Henri Poivelaine was still robbed this morning en route from Hong Kong to Haiphong. The incident occurred 30 miles from Aoyan. While the second mate was at the engine, he was suddenly surrounded by several armed thugs. Within minutes, the entire ship was under the control of the pirates, who first destroyed the wireless equipment and seized weapons, and then proceeded to loot. After finishing, they forced the captain to sail to Zhelangjiao. Upon arrival, the pirates fired at small boats, requisitioned two boats, and abducted four Chinese passengers along with 15,000 yuan worth of stolen goods. The robbed ship, with a tonnage of 1,355 tons, belongs to the French company, Xinji (transliteration). (26th Reuters Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The four Chinese passengers abducted from the French ship are Wu Qing (transliteration), a merchant from Haiphong; Zhang Xinbo, a former Chinese customs official; Lei Hexin (transliteration), a former Guangdong military officer; and Meng Guo (transliteration), a gambler from Guangdong. The captain told passengers that the pirates attacked unexpectedly. Four Annamese guards were stationed on the ship, three of whom were off duty. The one on duty was unable to resist and was captured by the pirates. The compradore, Qi Chang, hid in the cargo hold, and his assistant, Rong, hid in the coal bunker, but both were discovered by the pirates. The safe in the compradore's office was opened, and 800 yuan in cash was looted. When disembarking, the pirates drove the captain and sailors into a lifeboat and towed it away to prevent them from staying on the ship and ramming the pirates' small boats. The captain was beaten by a pirate but was not injured. The captain and others were later released by the pirates. Upon returning to the ship, they repaired the wireless equipment and sent out a distress signal. A British warship heard the alert and came to escort the ship to port. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The French ship Henri Livius, en route from Hong Kong to Haiphong, was robbed by pirates yesterday. The pirates disguised themselves as passengers and boarded the ship in Hong Kong. In the middle of the journey, they suddenly rose up and forced the captain to sail to Qilangjiao (transliteration), stealing ornaments and money totaling about 15,000 yuan and abducting four passengers. Hong Kong police had seen many pirates lingering in the port a few days ago and warned the ships, but they could not be arrested at that time because there was no formal case. (26th Kuomin Dispatch)

Current Commentary: The Turbulent Far Eastern Political Situation (Continued) (Yes) | The Future of the Chinese Market After the Resumption of Diplomatic Relations Between the United States and the Soviet Union | 47

The resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and the Soviet Union only indicates the increasing tension in the Far East. The impact of this is limited to making Japan's policy of invading China more roundabout and tortuous. The reason for this was briefly mentioned yesterday. However, under the extremely opposite political and economic positions of these two major countries, what impact will the changes in the economic control war within the Chinese market have after they join hands? It seems that it is also necessary to conduct considerable research. The root cause of today's Far East dispute lies in the inability of the imperialist powers to maintain the balance of power in the Far East market. The Pacific Mandate issue, the Indian market issue, etc., are all reflections of this phenomenon, but they are only local facts. The struggle for the right to control the Chinese market is the center of this fundamental problem. Japan has always regarded itself as the leader of East Asia. Even if the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and the Soviet Union may slightly restrain its ambition to aggressively invade territory, it will never be able to curb its disguised economic aggression. This can be asserted.

However, looking at today's Chinese market, which has long been in a state of being devoured by imperialist aggression, coupled with domestic unrest, has bankrupted our rural areas, made cities desolate, production has declined, and purchasing power is weak. The depth of suffering is undeniable. At this time, the general public has no power to save themselves, and the rural landlords and the bourgeoisie only feel that the prosperity is far away. It is very clear that this situation will inevitably fail to promote the beneficial development of the Chinese market. Countries with ambitions for aggression will see this as a good opportunity and more directly intensify their aggression, and more rapidly increase the economic conflicts between these countries. The economic control war within the Chinese market will inevitably become more and more intense.

Looking at recent events, Japan has expanded its basic industries in China, such as the textile and shipping industries, as much as possible, and has also organized a controlled trade agency for China, such as the so-called "Japan-China Trade Co., Ltd." Furthermore, it has established various direct sales agencies in the major trading ports of China. When merchants cannot afford it, they are supported by the government. This is the economic war formation that Japan has expressed towards China after all countries have unanimously resisted Japanese goods. As for Britain and the United States, since they are planning to resist Japanese goods in other markets, they will certainly not fall behind in the Chinese market. For example, the recent US movement to raise the price of silver, and the British Parliament's plan to revitalize the Chinese market, are all beginnings. From this point of view, the economic hegemony of various countries in the Chinese market will inevitably take a more direct and controlled form in the future. The contradiction between the economic forces of various countries will inevitably become more acute in the future. This is the new situation that we must recognize after the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and the Soviet Union, and before the armed struggle between various countries. Fellow countrymen, please think about it.

Mussolini Launches League of Nations Restructuring Movement: Seeking to Have the United States, Russia, Germany, and Japan Join to Save the Tense International Situation - Invitation to Litvinov to Visit Italy is Related to This 48

(London) The World News reported today that sources believe Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is launching a movement to expand the power of the League of Nations, seeking to have the United States, Russia, Japan, and Germany join the restructured League. Difficulties with the Japanese Budget Proposal; Navy Ministry's Attitude Quite Firm; Future of Political Situation Not Optimistic 54

The Army, Navy, and Agriculture and Forestry Ministries are particularly opposed to the Ministry of Finance. It is reported that the Army Ministry has slightly changed its attitude since yesterday, reducing its original request for 108 million yen to below 70 million yen to seek a compromise with the Ministry of Finance. The Agriculture and Forestry Ministry is requesting an additional 33 million yen, but the Ministry of Finance only approved 3 million yen. Minister of Agriculture and Forestry Goto, at yesterday's national internal affairs chiefs' conference, outlined the key points of the dispute between the Agriculture and Finance Ministries, implicitly seeking assistance from local officials to resolve rural issues. The attending internal affairs chiefs surprisingly resolved to urge the government to quickly resolve the anxieties of farmers' lives, restraining the financial authorities. However, the Navy Ministry still insists on its original proposal, so Finance Minister Takahashi plans to seek a political solution with Navy Minister Osumi, Army Minister Araki, and Agriculture and Forestry Minister Goto in the next two days, to implement his "national defense first" principle. Japanese fascists and military personnel are seizing the opportunity to begin activities. The other day, they used the name of Prince Konoe, Speaker of the House of Peers, to propagate that there would be a coup d'état on November 20. Recently, they have been propagating that the Saito Cabinet will step down by the end of the month due to the budget issue. The financial and economic communities are very uneasy. (Tokyo) The Seiyukai party is paying close attention to the development of the political situation centered on the budget. Anglo-Russian Trade Treaty Negotiations; Issue of Mining Compensation; Not Solvable in a Short Time 59

(London) Anglo-Russian trade treaty negotiations, which were stalled in April of this year due to the case of the employees of the Lena Goldfields Company, have recently resumed, with good prospects. Several issues have now been agreed upon. The greatest difficulty lies with the Lena Goldfields Company, which is seeking US$13 million in compensation from the Soviet Union for violating the mining concession granted in 1925. It is now believed that the British authorities are advocating setting the claim at £3.5 million, while the Russian side is only willing to pay £1 million. If this dispute can be settled on an agreed figure, the signing of a new treaty between the two countries will not be long delayed. (Reuters Telegram, 25th)

(London) Although Anglo-Russian trade negotiations have not reached a stalemate, they seem to be encountering various difficulties. The crux of the matter is the issue of Article 20 of the Ottawa Agreement. It now seems that it can be resolved on the following basis: that the United Kingdom cannot prohibit the import of Russian goods without giving three months' prior notice. As for the damages of £13,000,000 for the Lena Goldfields (a mine jointly operated by Russia and England in which British capital was confiscated), the Soviet representatives have not yet proposed any solution. The United Kingdom has also requested that the Soviet Union guarantee a corresponding proportion of British goods imported into Russia, according to the quantity of Russian goods imported into England. (Havas Telegram, 25th)

North China Under Active War Preparations by Japan and Russia; Japanese Troops Secretly Deployed to North Manchuria; Japanese Goods Dumped in North China to Absorb Cash; Japanese and Korean Ruffians Rampant in the War Zone; Puppet State Banknotes in Circulation as Far as Tangshan 72

Peiping Correspondence: The Japanese warlords are preparing to create a second world war. Their war preparation goals are to use the Navy to deal with Britain and the United States, and the Army to confront Soviet Russia. After the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia, the situation has changed dramatically. The Japanese military preparations have become even more active. On one hand, they are trying to resolve the Sino-Japanese issue to avoid being constrained in the rear, and on the other hand, they are increasing troops in North Manchuria to prevent any possible war. Most of the Japanese troops stationed along the Great Wall have already been moved north. Recently, they have again been transporting a large number of troops from Japan to Manchuria, landing at the port of Rajin, and transporting them to the Harbin area via Jilin. A large number of cavalry, artillery, and air force units have also been deployed to Manchuria Station, near the Russian border. Troop transportation is mostly done at night, and strict secrecy is maintained from the outside world. Information about North Manchuria is transmitted by air every day to ensure speed and avoid leakage. After the news of the Japanese aircraft suddenly flying into Russian territory on the 8th of this month was released, it was also rumored in the puppet state that Russian aircraft had once scouted the Harbin and Changchun areas. Japan and the puppet state are planning to move the capital of the puppet state to Lushun for safety reasons in case of war between Japan and Russia, because Changchun, the capital of the puppet state, is closer to the Russian border and is vulnerable to Russian aircraft attacks, so as to facilitate protection.

The Japanese authorities are desperately coping with this serious situation, but their financial and material resources are insufficient to meet the needs. Therefore, they regard the four northeastern provinces and North China as their only external treasury. For the four northeastern provinces, on the one hand, they are extracting resources through the puppet organization, and on the other hand, they are still using monetary policies to concentrate cash and promote gold notes (Japanese banknotes are called gold notes in the Northeast) as much as possible in the northeastern provinces, absorbing cash back to the country. Recently, due to the proliferation of gold notes and the extremely tight financial situation in the country, the price of gold notes in the northeastern provinces has fallen daily, with each yuan worth only 90 cents in silver. At the same time, the puppet state also issued puppet banknotes in the name of the puppet Central Bank. The banknotes are divided into several denominations, such as one yuan, five yuan, ten yuan, fifty yuan, one hundred yuan, five hundred yuan, and one thousand yuan, and there are also corner notes such as one jiao, two jiao, and five jiao. The puppet banknotes are printed by the Japanese. The national flag of the puppet state is printed on the upper right corner of the front, and two articles of the puppet state's monetary law are printed on the back, which is quite unique. A large number of puppet banknotes have been issued, flooding the market. Silver dollars have disappeared, and it has become a world of paper money. Affected by the war, the Japanese domestic industry is in recession, and factory output exceeds demand. All the circulating capital has become stagnant output. Under this economic downturn, each factory and businessman must also do their best for national use in preparation for the war. They have no choice but to regard the Northeast and North China as their tail, implementing the dumping of goods. In recent months, Japanese goods imported into North China have increased dramatically. The markets in Peiping and Tianjin are flooded with Japanese goods, and the prices are lower than ever before. General merchants, greedy for profit, are competing to sell them, and the sales of Japanese goods have become very widespread, and the resources transferred to the enemy are also countless. At the same time, the Japanese army is using force to protect Japanese and Korean ruffians, selling drugs, harming our people, and absorbing our money. Local authorities know this but cannot prohibit it. Even an occasional intervention will lead to negotiations. It is even more unbearable to ask about the situation within the war zone. Because it is under the power of the Japanese army, everything is controlled by the Japanese army. Puppet banknotes are now circulating as far as Tangshan. Therefore, North China is now the same as the Northeast before the September 18th Incident. The future is truly unimaginable. (November 25th)

North China; All Armies Will Be Downsized Again; Due to Extreme Difficulties with Military Spending 73

Peiping Correspondence: Although military spending in North China has been reduced repeatedly, it still requires 4,965,000 yuan per month as of now. The budget for formal troops is 4,520,000 yuan. After the Chahar incident is resolved, the incorporated miscellaneous troops will cost approximately 440,000 yuan. However, of the military spending in North China, in addition to the 3.5 million yuan allocated by the Central Government each month, 850,000 yuan is reported by Hebei, Chahar, and Peiping, and 210,000 yuan is reported by the Peiping-Liaoning and Peiping-Suiyuan Railways and Tianjin to help. However, since Hebei and Chahar provinces were ravaged by war, local finances have also been difficult. Therefore, they have stopped reporting one after another, and the troops' salaries are only supported by the subsidy allocated by the Central Government, with a large difference each month. Therefore, only the sixth salary has been paid, and when the seventh salary can be paid is still far away. The Central Government and local authorities owe the Military Affairs Commission a total of 8,210,000 yuan as of the end of July, and this does not include the amount owed since August. At the routine meeting of the Military Affairs Commission the other day, the generals had a long discussion on this issue. The opinions can be summarized into three points: (1) The living expenses of the armies will be changed to monthly salary payments; (2) The central subsidy will be distributed equally first; (3) Borrowing will be used to provide assistance first, and the balance will be paid off at the end of the month, but none of these are appropriate solutions, so they dispersed without any results. In the intention of the authorities, the current finances in North China are depleted, and military spending is huge. If relief measures are not taken as soon as possible, the future will be very dangerous. Therefore, they still hope that the provinces and cities can continue to do their best to assist, and they plan to make every effort to downsize the armies again. However, this method is complicated and is currently being carefully planned. In addition to military spending, disaster relief matters in the war zone also urgently need to be carried out in North China. The North China War Zone Agricultural Relief Group has now started to provide loans for agricultural relief in Zunhua, Fengrun, and Xuanhua counties, and last week sent personnel to Huairou, Miyun, Pinggu, Ji County, and Qian'an counties to conduct investigations. Once the investigation is completed, cooperatives will be organized to implement loans. According to Zhang Yuanshan, head of the Agricultural Relief Group, the agricultural relief work of this association should have started earlier, but the relief funds have not been allocated, which has delayed the full handling of the matter. However, this work cannot be delayed for too long, so the 130,000 yuan of relief funds raised by donations has been used to start the investigation and loan work in the eight counties of Xuanhua, etc. He estimated that the agricultural relief work will be completed before February of next year. Regarding the issuance of war zone public bonds, the North China War Zone Relief Committee is scheduled to convene a meeting of standing committee members this Saturday to discuss and consult on the issuance methods. The issuance procedures for public bonds are roughly divided into three stages: (1) Organizing a management committee; (2) Printing public bond tickets; (3) Contacting the banking industry to promote sales. It is estimated that after this standing committee meeting, the war zone public bonds can be issued and will not be affected by any parties. The agricultural relief portion of the relief funds is planned to be 300,000 yuan in public bond tickets. If these public bonds can be sold out in a short period of time, the agricultural relief progress will not be hindered. According to Zhang, emergency relief work has now been completed in four-fifths, so it has been decided to complete the work by the end of this month. (23rd)

Lu Antiquities Research Association to Excavate the Ancient Capital of the Zhu State; Excavations at Anshang Village and the Tomb of Cao Wang Have Been Completed 75

Jinan Correspondence: Dong Zuobin of the Shandong Antiquities Research Association and others have completed their excavation of Anshang Village and the Tomb of Cao Wang in Teng County. They discovered divination turtle shells, pottery shards, clam tools, stone tools, Han Dynasty stone carvings, human bones, etc., which are commonly found elsewhere and have no special value. The work has now ended. Wang Xiantang, director of the Shandong Provincial Library (Wang is also a member of the Shandong Antiquities Research Association), went to Teng County to meet with Dong Zuobin to discuss going to Zou County to conduct a survey in preparation for excavating the ancient capital of the Jiwangcheng ancient Da Zhu state, searching for the culture of the Spring and Autumn period. The Zhu state of the Spring and Autumn period was later divided into three. The capitals of the Lan and Xiao Zhu states were both in Teng County. The Zhu state (i.e., Da Zhu) was in Zou County. Jiwangcheng, more than twenty li south of Mount Yi in Zou County, is its capital. (According to the ancient pronunciation, Ji is Zhi, which is the transliteration of Zhu.) Many bronze artifacts have been found there before. Most of the archaeological bronze artifacts are unearthed here, with dozens of types recorded. Furthermore, pottery shards with writing are often found in the county, which are quite valuable. In our country, pottery shards with writing have been found only in Shaanxi and Shandong. In Shaanxi, the culture of the Qin state can be studied. In Shandong, there are Zibo and Zou County. There are many characters on the pottery shards in Zibo, which can be used to study the culture of the Qi state. There are fewer characters on the pottery shards in Zou County, which can be used to study the culture of the Zhu state. In recent years, after rain in the fields of Zou County, they have often been discovered. Children sell them to people for rescue. The above-mentioned bronze artifacts and pottery shards with writing are all in an important position in the archaeological world. It is expected that the value of future excavations will be above that of the Anshang Village Cao Wang tomb. (24th)

Liu Zhi Returns to Bianliang, Discusses the Inspection Tour of Wushe and Lin Counties 76

Kaifeng Correspondence: Liu Zhi left Bianliang on the 15th for northern Henan, inspecting engineering projects in the Zhengzhou Miaogong area. After inspecting Wuzhi, Daokou, and Huaxian, he took a special train north from Xinxiang to Handan, disembarked, and turned west to inspect Wu'an, Shexian, and Linxian. He returned by train from Zhangde, stopped briefly in Zhengzhou, and returned to Bianliang this afternoon. According to his account, the mountain roads from Wu'an to Shexian and Linxian are rugged, and cars cannot travel on them. The Zhang River winds around, sometimes climbing mountains, sometimes wading through water. Among them, Qingfeng Mountain in Shexian has cliffs and steep walls, and transportation is particularly inconvenient. Even sedan chairs and horses cannot be used. Therefore, in five days, he only traveled three hundred and twenty li. The highways in the three counties, Shexian and Linxian, have only been partially built. Wu'an is currently starting construction. These three counties are located in the northwest corner of Henan, bordering Hebei and Shanxi. The mountains are precipitous, and the roads are dangerous. Wu'an has many merchants doing business outside, so the economy is quite sufficient. However, customs are extravagant, and both men and women like to dress up. In Shexian and Linxian, because there are many mountains and little land, people's livelihoods are difficult. Many people use bran and persimmon fruits, ground into crumbs to fill their hunger. The people of Shexian are simple and honest, while the people of Linxian are contentious and fond of fighting. However, the Tianmen Society bandits have long been suppressed, and social order is stable. Although the bad customs of keeping queues, foot binding, and superstition have not been eliminated, education is still developed, and political achievements are also good. However, the prevalence of drugs is a major disaster in these three counties. The flood in Huaxian is extremely serious. The fifth, sixth, and seventh districts are almost completely submerged, with only one village remaining in the fifth district with one hundred and twenty-six villages, three villages remaining in the sixth district with one hundred and fifty-three villages, and two villages remaining in the seventh district with one hundred and sixty-three villages. The land has turned into a swamp, and it is still a vast expanse of water. Dozens of miles around Baliying, Anshang Village, and Nanyangliu and other villages are submerged in water with broken tiles and crumbling walls. Hundreds of thousands of disaster victims are crying for food and shivering from the cold, homeless. County Chief Xie Suian has selected male and female disaster victims with farming ability, quickly investigated and reported, in order to move them to the special zone in southern Henan, it is said. (23rd)

Feng Yuxiang Has No Connection with the Fujian Incident; Unwilling to Participate in Any Political Occasions Again; Still Practicing Calligraphy and Reading Books Every Day in Mount Tai 77

Taian Correspondence: After the Fujian Incident occurred, Feng Yuxiang, who was residing in Mount Tai, attracted considerable attention from the people of the country. It was rumored that Feng had some contact with the Fujian uprising. The major reasons were: 1. Xu Qian, who once served as Feng's representative, is currently an important figure in Fujian; 2. According to a certain source, Feng was recommended by Fujian as a member of the new government. In fact, Feng did not seem to approve of the Fujian side's measures. It is said that representatives from Fujian had visited Feng in Mount Tai beforehand. Feng stated that since returning to Mount Tai, he was merely one of the common people and did not want to participate in any political occasions again. He only hoped to have the opportunity to read and practice calligraphy every day, which he felt was sufficient. Feng's guards in Mount Tai originally numbered one thousand five hundred, but four to five hundred people were recently laid off and dismissed separately. Currently, there are about one thousand people remaining. Feng's daily expenses are supplemented by Song Zheyuan and Han Fuqu, so he does not feel it is too difficult. Feng practices calligraphy and reads books every day in the mountains. He rarely receives guests other than his former subordinates. Feng does not express his opinions on the current situation. Recently, he has had no intention of going to Beijing. The rumor that the Central Government invited Feng to Beijing is not true. When asked about the Fujian incident, he stated that he had only seen it in the newspapers and had not heard the details. The rumor that he participated is purely untrue, it is said. (24th)
