This family quarrel was the prelude to Mr. Li's unfortunate incident. Mrs. Li and her children, after suffering losses that day, cried every day, secretly plotting revenge. Mrs. Li came up with a method of using force, spending a lot of money to hire a large group of hooligans to harass the concubine. Who knew that when the hooligans came to吵鬧, the dissolute woman had Mr. Li's protection, so she couldn't be harmed at all. All that was achieved was the loss of her husband's reputation and the mess of the family!

Although Mrs. Li's plan failed, her husband became even more hostile towards her! In addition to scolding her all day long, he also used harsh and vicious methods to stop providing food and expenses for her and her children. So Mrs. Li became even more悲痛, feeling that her husband was using such a vicious means of cutting off the source of their livelihood to压迫, and that the feelings between husband and wife had long been completely lost. So, why should she care about the overall situation? Therefore, on a certain night last month, she secretly gathered her belongings, took her children, and slipped away in the night to the city, where she went to the judiciary to sue her husband for smoking opium, requesting a speedy investigation and arrest. The authorities had long been jealous of Mr. Li's wealth and opium smoking. Now that Mrs. Li went to sue, it was a chance of財星高照, a highly desirable opportunity. They immediately sent twelve bailiffs with a document to 李's house. At that time, Mr. Li was on the opium couch,偎着 his lover, smiling happily and庆幸 that his wife's departure was like removing a thorn in his side.

He and the dissolute woman were caught by the bailiffs along with evidence and witnesses and taken back to the court, where they were detained in prison. In the iron cage, he learned that this matter was done by his wife, and he was very angry in his heart. But then he thought that he should not have used such a vicious means to stop the source of livelihood for her and her children. As the saying goes, "If he has feelings, I will have righteousness." So it is no wonder that she used this vicious plan to retaliate! However, it was too late for him to realize this and repent.

Alas! Because of a "concubine," the feelings between husband and wife broke down, the ethics between father and son were destroyed, and a happy family was torn apart, which is unthinkable. How sad! So the saying that concubines are a "source of trouble" is not a slanderous term.

The sun shines on the rice in the field, reflecting a golden color. A slight breeze has brought the chill of early winter. People in the village are all harvesting rice in the field, which is the richest time in the countryside in deep autumn.

Shanghai (4) 258

— Zhang Lao San

(7) Sister's Soul

Besides my parents in heaven, my lovely brother hundreds of miles away, I also have sympathetic enemies. The new beginning did not disappoint me. Ying Li's future shone with a line of light. I regained my sister Min, my loving sister Min.

When I was ten years old, during the Yuan宵 Festival, my father bought three走馬燈. The sky was not dark yet. I lit the candle and siblings ran around everywhere. We偷门门口, the streets were full of people, carrying all kinds of lamps,欢跃,狂笑, we stood in front of a familiar shop, a cluster of people擁 from afar, mixed voices shouted to see the dragon lantern, the crowd came like a tide, we couldn't avoid it, siblings were rolled away. I was walking while shouting loudly sister Min, at this time no one noticed a lost sister's child crying and shouting, I was crowded on the side of the road, there was a familiar person took me home.

I received a heavy责打 from my parents, and from then on I lost my loving sister Min, now my sister's soul has descended on the naughty child. "I am sister Min," this powerful little voice gave me more courage.

I stared at sister Min's face, sister Min stared at me, the room maintained each other's understanding of joy, in the hearts of two异乡,激荡 up the victory of凯旋.

(8) Shanghai in Spring

Walking back from the dining room, Shanghai was full of lively air, every smiling shadow shone in the light of the neon lights. The window decorations on Nanjing Road seduced the attention of passers-by. "Dream Lover" was情地 broadcast from the radio, and the huang包夫 also released their轻郁 footsteps, pulling their customers to their destinations. In Shanghai, it seems that no sad faces can be seen. We jumped back to the hotel.

Relying on the洋台, looking far into the misty hometown, I remembered my lovely brother.

"Sister Min, we have come to Shanghai to endure hardship, not to enjoy ourselves. Living in such a noble hotel is too far from our purpose in Shanghai. Our first question is丨a quiet apartment. A亭子楼 is also good. We have to start from the bottom!"

"Brother, forgive me for deceiving you to such a hotel. I have a friend, who is the principal of the kindergarten. Not long ago, she wrote to me to ask me to share her a job, let me first restore my音心, sort out my soul. You, first see your舅舅, how much he can help you, don't you think that capitalists have no sympathy. Since yesterday, this nerve恍, you didn't sleep on the train, did you, muttering to yourself, I'm really afraid you want to commit suicide, sleep, Shanghai 本天, it's still斜寒 attacking at night".

"Sister Min, I辜负 your kindness, forgive me, for calling you a soulless woman".

Closed the long window, I took off my clothes and slept稳了, sister Min才退身 out. Fatigue is indeed fatigue, but being stimulated by a certain inexplicable and excited thing, using the hypnotic method of counting one two three four, the number increased by itself, staring blankly at the top of the account with no sleep. 乱 的思潮, even映 like a movie: friends after graduation are lost, a person was遣弃 land back to his hometown, hometown for me and no恋 of the place, the tombs of two old people, the river under the bridge, in addition to the lovely younger brother, I would not mention any person and any thing. I deeply sucked a mouth of smoke, opened the long window.

Movie Special

A Glimpse of Scenery and People in Bali, Nanyang 259

— Translated by Xi Fu

American gold has raised the local cost of living, leaving people from other countries with a sense of helpless longing.

I remember a few years ago, an Austrian painter of oil paintings arrived in Shanghai. Through a friend's introduction, I visited him at his residence to admire his works from Bali Island in the South Seas. I had long heard of Bali, and in my mind, it held the same allure as Hawaii, making me yearn to go there. This was because of its beautiful mountains and rivers, its elegant people, and, to be honest, especially the "natural and unadorned" women who didn't wear tops. However, the artist gave me a deeper understanding. None of his works featured nude women; instead, they were all portraits of dignified women with their faces front and center. In his works, I felt that the beauty of Balinese women's faces surpassed that of women in any other country, incomparable to modern women adorned with fragrance and rouge. Comparing women with painted faces to the natural beauty of Bali is like comparing clay and wooden idols to the solemn and exquisite appearance of the Jade Buddha of Tuancheng.

But what does this have to do with movies? My thoughts arose from a piece of news. I heard that Hollywood had sent people to Bali to film a movie entirely capturing the local scenery and customs. I was delighted by the hope that we would soon see Bali's people and landscapes on the silver screen. However, our country doesn't want to overly promote things beforehand, so the title of the film, etc., will not be mentioned for now.

Everyone probably knows the name of the Nanyang Islands, which are called the South Seas in English. This area is not far from China. The largest island there is called Borneo, which is a British territory. Further south are Java, Bali, and other places, all part of the Dutch East Indies. Many Chinese people do business and trade there, controlling a significant portion of the commercial power. However, that place, especially Bali, is not well-known by Westerners, so apart from the locals and Chinese people, few Westerners travel there. It is said that five years ago, on average, only about seventy Europeans and Americans visited Bali each season. However, now, the number of Europeans and Americans traveling there has increased to as many as fifteen hundred per season. As a result, the Dutch government has made a great fortune in the tourism business.

We all know that the Dutch government makes money from its colonies, and this is especially true for Bali. Bali Island is where the Dutch government sold the patent rights there to a company, and the Queen of the Netherlands is one of the largest shareholders of that company. Since Americans discovered the scenery and people of that place, they have regarded it as a paradise and gone there to travel, especially Hollywood stars. Since Americans flaunted their gold there, the standard of living there has risen to the extreme, as high as the temperature. Perhaps wealthy people from Britain and France can still go there to appreciate the topless girls. People from other countries may only be able to sigh in admiration from afar. It is said that even the Dutch themselves are unwilling to go because the prices are too high.

Many Hollywood stars have traveled there. Among the most famous are Charlie Chaplin, Douglas Fairbanks, and others. There is a joke that when Charlie Chaplin and his brother Syd arrived there, the local Dutch government, for some reason, treated them as if two emperors had descended, inviting them to play and dine every day, which made them both laugh and cry and caused them stomach problems. Later, fortunately, an old friend rescued them and hid them in a remote place on the edge of the island, where they recovered from their stomach ailments. Currently, Gloria Swanson and her husband Henry, as well as Constance Bennett and others, are vacationing in Bali.

Film Reviews

Review of "Fragrant Vanilla Beauty" 260

— Ling He

丨Mingxing Production丨New Guang Premiere丨

First of all, we must acknowledge that the author has adopted realistic subject matter and has accurately grasped and analyzed it, which is indeed commendable.

Rural bankruptcy and the constant flow of rural men and women into cities and factories are inevitable phenomena. However, so-called national capital ultimately cannot withstand the invasion of foreign capital and fails after exhausting all its efforts in competition. At the same time, although national capital succumbs to the economic or political power of foreign countries, it also squeezes and exploits workers as much as possible. As a result, workers are hungry and suffering, and after factories close, the number of unemployed people in society increases daily. At this time, enlightened people struggle and fight for their livelihoods. In contrast, "pure and honest" workers! Their adherence to their place leads them to recognize their own way out after extreme torment.

Overall, we largely agree with the playwright's statement, but the compassion for national capital and the subsequent depiction of workers living in dire straits due to exploitation inevitably reveals a contradiction in the author's emotions. In our works, we should certainly depict the inevitable decline of national capital, but excessive sympathy weakens the audience's emotions, which cannot but be a loss, right? It is said that the script for this film was written by a Fudan University student, which makes it even more interesting. Indeed, Chinese films have been widely noticed by the general public, and with this new trend and good results, it further proves the greatness of the future of Chinese cinema.

In terms of performance, director Chen Kengran's use of the interplay between the present and memories is a new method in China. However, we feel that it is used too much, which makes people find it fragmented and disrupts the unity of the mood, like a running account. For example, when Wang Ada says in court, "Another three years have passed like this," or "One night," and then immediately illustrates it with a picture, it is undoubtedly a convenient method for the performance, but if the scenes are organized and tightly woven together, it is not impossible, and the audience's emotions will be more compact and unified. We believe that the opening courtroom scene, which changes from the policeman's mouth to the scene, until Ada says, "I am a carpenter..." and then continues with the scene to the end, and finally ends this memory in the courtroom, seems relatively good. Moreover, one episode of past events and another of courtroom scenes eventually become annoying. Moreover, there are too many explanatory subtitles.

Apart from this, we must admit that the director has made considerable use of new methods. The characterization of Wang Ada's daughter, played by Xia Peizhen, using perfume, new cheongsams, and learning to smoke cigarettes to explain her later bold selling of her body, the depiction of Ada's brother, played by Wang Weixin, as daring to be angry but not daring to speak out when drinking tea at work to illustrate his rebellious personality, and the depiction of Ada, played by Xie Yunqing, as being cautious and representing the typical figure of the feudal era, as well as the choice of other actors, such as Ada's wife as the pure virtuous wife (her elopement with her daughter is a bit odd), and the child's malnutrition, are all very good.

It should also be pointed out that the night scene outside the window, from night to dawn, discovering that the daughter has brought a man home because of her cigarette, the riotous scene in the factory, the scene of the police catching Ada and his brother, burning cakes, and Ada teasing his child, are all very good. In particular, the depiction of Wang Ada's family is full of genuine Chinese living habits. The "cartoon" of gold yuan toppling Chinese chimneys is also good.

However, there are also some minor shortcomings: the depiction of Ada's wife running away lacks sufficient foreshadowing, resulting in oddness. Many shots in the playground take up too much time. The scene of Ada taking the child to the hospital can be omitted, but the scene of the return journey is meaningful. At the same time, the emotions of the tragedy are not strong enough, which should be due to the disruption of the courtroom scene mentioned earlier, because the feeling cannot be concentrated.

Now let's talk about the actors. Xie Yunqing's performance is simply amazing. He failed so badly in "Iron Plate Red Tears Record," but he is so successful here. He has such a good grasp of the character's emotions and personality. He deserves the greatest credit for the success of this film. Xia Peizhen comes down from the stairs slowly buttoning her collar, which is very natural, but there is no progress compared to the past. In particular, her head makeup is even more unsuitable. Wang Weixin has performed much better than before. Since he began to play rebellious roles in "Iron Plate Red Tears Record," he has shown his success here. The best is naturally the scene of drinking tea.

Although the cinematography is not brilliant, it is still acceptable, which is not surprising in a large company. The sets have made the same mistake as before, such as the courtroom and the hospital, which are so modern that they always feel too distant. Why should we work so hard on the sets to exaggerate the plot unnecessarily? I hope the decorators of the Mingxing Company will pay special attention.

Review of "Healthy Women" 261

— Li Fu

According to the writer's limited knowledge, this is the first "pure cultural film" without a story to be shown in Shanghai. Although the "Maternity Hygiene Film," which was shown at the Japanese Arts Hall on North Sichuan Road a few years ago and was rumored by Shanghai people at the time to be a model film, can be said to be a type of cultural film, there is a considerable distance between a purely objective "documentary film" and a "cultural film" with positive educational significance.

Although it was not stated in the newspaper which country it was produced in, anyone who pays a little attention to the state of world cultural films knows that this is a work by the Soviet Mezhrabpom-Rus. It is funny that when a Soviet film is released, they use words like "Italian Mussolini, German Hitler Awards" for publicity. In fact, in Germany, all Soviet films, including cultural films, have long been banned by the Hitler government.

This film is a work edited and filmed under a certain purpose consciousness, using documentary film methods and adding many clever diagrams. In order to adjust the audience's interest, several obvious contrasts are interspersed in the middle. For example, the Mongolian people's habit of childbirth, which is unattended and makes people laugh, is compared with all the equipment of the Soviet government's labor women's maternity hospital. This not only effectively achieves the purpose of education, but also leads to a deep reflection on the kind of social organization that can make all women perform their maternal duties so comfortably and peacefully.

We saw the sanitary equipment of the factory female workers. After working for a few hours, the female workers happily opened all the windows, took off their work clothes, and neatly held five minutes of flexibility.

It almost made me suspect that this was the same as Lili Li teaching poor children to do gymnastics in "Little Toys," which is a kind of author's fantasy; a viewer behind me was whispering: "This is something that can't be done in practice." It is true that this cannot be done in China or Europe, America, and Japan, but what is shown in this film is the Soviet Union under another social order. There is a famous saying: "When a film is in the hands of ignorant deceivers, it will not only fail to benefit the audience, but will also spread harmful seeds to them, but when the audience themselves have obtained the film, when the film is grasped in the hands of the real activists of the new culture, it will become one of the most powerful tools of mass education." "Healthy Women" proves the correctness of this sentence. This film can bring many benefits to the audience, whether in terms of knowledge or understanding.

Comparing this film with those films that are made for profit and cause the audience to have bad reactions, I think the smart audience will definitely get a clear answer.

Our Jin Yan is Actually Like This! 262

— He

It's strange, I met Jin Yan on Avenue Joffre. Why is it strange? There is no reason for it. For me, it was a chance encounter. Haven't we been out of touch for a long time? Now we have met again.

I saw him wearing a red wool jacket, golf pants, and a primary school student's hat on his head. His complexion was not very healthy, a typical yellow race. We shook hands once. I said:

"I saw the announcement you posted in the newspaper. What's going on?"

"This, it's a joke. Someone sees me as an important figure in a certain party or faction. This is simply exaggerating me too much. In fact, I am ignorant and have no skills. I am ashamed that I can only make women happy on the screen. So I posted an announcement to tell the truth."

"Ah, this is really... too... too... what is it (it's always painful when someone can't express themselves). But why would someone suspect you?"

"This is probably because I played Carmen at the Nanguo Society." He added: "But this is also a very simple matter. Tian Han asked Wan Laitian to find me to help perform in a play. I did it because I liked it. In fact, I have no real friendship with Tian Han. I don't even know where his house is."

"Well, this is funny... " I asked again. "So, is it easy for people to misunderstand you when you act in films like "The Light of Motherhood" and "Three Modern Women"?"

"Brother, there is nothing I can do about it. To be honest, I am an actor. I signed a contract with the company. If the company wants me to play a certain role, can I refuse? If they want me to be a traitor who sells out the country, I have to do it."

"Let's not talk about these things... How is your life recently?"

"My life is quite interesting. I study vocal music on Wednesdays and Saturdays. In addition, I play ball, do the horizontal bar, use powder, watch movies, and also like to hunt. Speaking of this, I have to say it again. Everyone must recognize the face of a movie actor. There is no way for me to be secretive anywhere. How can someone like me be fit to carry out secret activities?"

"Oh! I see."

A car drove up and separated us, so I waved to him and said:

"You go yours, I have to go back."

Film Novels Bring Glory to the Country (2) 263

— Xie Yuesheng

"Sister, he just came from the city," Hongyu quickly interjected to defend Tianxiong, and at the same time threw a wink at her brother, deliberately showing Xuefang the vest. "Sister: Look, he just bought this from the city." She fairly explained it for her brother. Xuefang felt that she had spoken too rashly, and a blush immediately appeared on her face. Tianxiong was also afraid that she would misunderstand, so he told her the news he heard in the city. He told Xuefang that an art exhibition would be held by West Lake tomorrow, and invited her to visit it together tomorrow. Xuefang agreed very readily.

The next morning, Xuefang and Tianxiong and Hongyu visited the works of the artist Su Rong at the exhibition. Su Rong personally received them. He was a young and promising artist, with a suave manner and gentle speech. Xuefang, who had a high sense of aesthetic appreciation, experienced a drastic rebellion in the depths of her heart after this acquaintance. She told him her address, saying that there were only an old mother and a weak sister at home. Su Rong, who was lonely in a foreign land, was of course very happy to receive this unexpected encounter. "Mr. Su, please come to my house when you are free, goodbye!" Xuefang, Tianxiong, and Hongyu bid farewell to Su Rong, and Su Rong personally sent them out.

"Is Miss Mei here too?" This voice stunned Xuefang and the others. So everyone turned their attention to this person, only to see the man swaggering over. Xuefang recognized him as Cao Huairen, a local gentleman with great wealth and power, but she disliked his arrogant and rude behavior, reluctantly greeted him, and left on her own. Cao Huairen relied on the omnipotence of money and implemented his pursuit work. After a few days, Cao Huairen specially bought many gifts to visit Mei Xuefang.

"She is ill, the doctor said she can't see guests," Cao Huairen was turned away. But he didn't suspect her, he just came out disappointed. Isn't this the young artist Su Rong from the exhibition that day? Cao Huairen saw Su Rong walking into the Mei house, and suddenly realized the situation when he was turned away. He decided to go in and find out the truth.

"Oh, are you Mr. Su? Please sit down! My daughter is inside." Huairen heard the voice of the speaker, who was the middle-aged woman who had just spoken to him. So his breathing became short and his hands and feet trembled a bit. He knew that the young artist was undoubtedly his rival in love. He couldn't bear to listen anymore, so he quietly retreated. He took a breath outside and walked away in frustration. Coincidentally, Hongyu and Tianxiong came to visit Xuefang, and when she saw Cao Huairen coming out of the inside, she hurriedly said to Tianxiong: "Brother: Look, how come that person is here to see Miss Mei too?"

"I don't think he is a good person, how does Miss Mei also interact with him?" They both thought the same way, and had already gone to the Mei house. (To be continued)
